demant s graduate programme global business working demant meet our employee graduate programme about u welcome to demant s graduate programme we offer you a career in a global medical healthcare company where you can look forward to an open and fun work environment a look our graduate film to get a first impression demant graduate programme youtube about demant demant is an international leading c company within hearing healthcare we operate in a global market with company in more than country our product are sold in more than country and we employee worldwide demant generates an annual revenue of dkk billion and cover five business activity hearing instrument hearing implant diagnostic equipment hearing care and personal communication about the programme the demant graduate programme offer you a unique opportunity to develop your personal and professional skill each year we hire between graduate different business area we will lead you through a two year journey starting in september depending on the business area you will different rotation each lasting month this will provide you with a broad understanding of our business and a network of people across function you will plan your rotation together with your host manager to enhance your development in the best possible way the programme also adapts to the need of the business therefore the project and task vary from rotation to rotation a we are a global company many of our graduate can also go abroad one of their rotation what else is in it you you will be given real task and responsibility with high exposure from day one we believe this is the best way to kick start your career after successfully completing the programme you will continue your career in demant in a permanent position we a flat organization which help you to get a holistic overview of our business to easier find your way around former graduate will partner up with you to support you we furthermore offer you training session such a project and stakeholder management skill we also offer a mentoring scheme which will focus on your personal development besides that you will join a fantastic network with the other graduate whereby everybody grows together already after the first day your business area global business in demant we the full value chain from idea and development to direct sale to our user a a graduate in global business you will work within our largest business where we are responsible operating a leading global hearing aid retailer our headquarters in smørum you will be a part of a highly dedicated and specialized team with a global outreach where we plan manage and execute a wide range of strategic and day to day activity our international colleague in our own hearing care shop around the world during your time in global business you will explore the company and develop your personal and professional skill through job rotation of month each there is a possibility to one of your rotation one of our location abroad the project you will be responsible will be anchored in current and need driven development and your own competency and interest project and task may include digital marketing analytics financial analysis m a customer journey strategy and it development and deployment we a focus on improving interface between business and it technology and how we on one hand can draw on that to enhance customer experience when they visit our shop and the same time optimize work process our colleague a a graduate you will be included in the day to day operation of the department where you also will direct exposure to top management in demant irrespective of the task one thing is certain you will face a steep learning curve with a high degree of responsibility from day one in our flat organization you will train your analytical strategic and innovative skill you will be exposed to a huge range of project you will be expected to take ownership your decision and to challenge status quo your profile you are about to graduate or graduated no more than two year ago with a master s degree in finance economics it accounting or strategy preferably a cand merc cand oecon or similar regardless of your educational background you a good commercial and technological understanding and want to explore the opportunity to optimize process through it you are a top performer with excellent achievement in either your study through your work experience or extracurricular activity you furthermore gained international experience through a semester or internship abroad or similar and last you are fluent in english a a person we believe that you are a team player with a high drive and passion what you do you are curious hardworking and just a important you are humble and fun to work with you are both strategic and pragmatic and go the ambitious goal how to apply please attach the following document to your online application cv master diploma if already hand max word word document answering the following question what will a great day a a graduate demant look like you deadline application is th of january we will then choose applicant video interview which take place from th st january after that we choose the final candidate our assessment center which take place on wednesday th of january our headquarters in smørum personal interview with the very last candidate graduate programme about u welcome to demant s graduate programme we offer you a career in a global medical healthcare company where you can look forward to an open and fun work environment a look our graduate film to get a first impression demant graduate programme youtube about demant demant is an international leading c company within hearing healthcare we operate in a global market with company in more than country our product are sold in more than country and we employee worldwide demant generates an annual revenue of dkk billion and cover five business activity hearing instrument hearing implant diagnostic equipment hearing care and personal communication about the programme the demant graduate programme offer you a unique opportunity to develop your personal and professional skill each year we hire between graduate different business area we will lead you through a two year journey starting in september depending on the business area you will different rotation each lasting month this will provide you with a broad understanding of our business and a network of people across function you will plan your rotation together with your host manager to enhance your development in the best possible way the programme also adapts to the need of the business therefore the project and task vary from rotation to rotation a we are a global company many of our graduate can also go abroad one of their rotation what else is in it you you will be given real task and responsibility with high exposure from day one we believe this is the best way to kick start your career after successfully completing the programme you will continue your career in demant in a permanent position we a flat organization which help you to get a holistic overview of our business to easier find your way around former graduate will partner up with you to support you we furthermore offer you training session such a project and stakeholder management skill we also offer a mentoring scheme which will focus on your personal development besides that you will join a fantastic network with the other graduate whereby everybody grows together already after the first day your business area global business in demant we the full value chain from idea and development to direct sale to our user a a graduate in global business you will work within our largest business where we are responsible operating a leading global hearing aid retailer our headquarters in smørum you will be a part of a highly dedicated and specialized team with a global outreach where we plan manage and execute a wide range of strategic and day to day activity our international colleague in our own hearing care shop around the world during your time in global business you will explore the company and develop your personal and professional skill through job rotation of month each there is a possibility to one of your rotation one of our location abroad the project you will be responsible will be anchored in current and need driven development and your own competency and interest project and task may include digital marketing analytics financial analysis m a customer journey strategy and it development and deployment we a focus on improving interface between business and it technology and how we on one hand can draw on that to enhance customer experience when they visit our shop and the same time optimize work process our colleague a a graduate you will be included in the day to day operation of the department where you also will direct exposure to top management in demant irrespective of the task one thing is certain you will face a steep learning curve with a high degree of responsibility from day one in our flat organization you will train your analytical strategic and innovative skill you will be exposed to a huge range of project you will be expected to take ownership your decision and to challenge status quo your profile you are about to graduate or graduated no more than two year ago with a master s degree in finance economics it accounting or strategy preferably a cand merc cand oecon or similar regardless of your educational background you a good commercial and technological understanding and want to explore the opportunity to optimize process through it you are a top performer with excellent achievement in either your study through your work experience or extracurricular activity you furthermore gained international experience through a semester or internship abroad or similar and last you are fluent in english a a person we believe that you are a team player with a high drive and passion what you do you are curious hardworking and just a important you are humble and fun to work with you are both strategic and pragmatic and go the ambitious goal how graduate programme about u welcome to demant s graduate programme we offer you a career in a global medical healthcare company where you can look forward to an open and fun work environment a look our graduate film to get a first impression demant graduate programme youtube about demant demant is an international leading c company within hearing healthcare we operate in a global market with company in more than country our product are sold in more than country and we employee worldwide demant generates an annual revenue of dkk billion and cover five business activity hearing instrument hearing implant diagnostic equipment hearing care and personal communication about the programme the demant graduate programme offer you a unique opportunity to develop your personal and professional skill each year we hire between graduate different business area we will lead you through a two year journey starting in september depending on the business area you will different rotation each lasting month this will provide you with a broad understanding of our business and a network of people across function you will plan your rotation together with your host manager to enhance your development in the best possible way the programme also adapts to the need of the business therefore the project and task vary from rotation to rotation a we are a global company many of our graduate can also go abroad one of their rotation what else is in it you you will be given real task and responsibility with high exposure from day one we believe this is the best way to kick start your career after successfully completing the programme you will continue your career in demant in a permanent position we a flat organization which help you to get a holistic overview of our business to easier find graduate programme about u welcome to demant s graduate programme we offer you a career in a global medical healthcare company where you can look forward to an open and fun work environment a look our graduate film to get a first impression demant graduate programme youtube about demant demant is an international leading c company within hearing healthcare we operate in a global market with company in more than country our product are sold in more than country and we employee worldwide demant generates an annual revenue of dkk billion and cover five business activity hearing instrument hearing implant diagnostic equipment hearing care and personal communication about the programme the demant graduate programme offer you a unique opportunity to develop your personal and professional skill each year we hire between graduate different business area we will lead you through a two year journey starting in september depending on the business area you will different rotation each lasting month this will provide you with a broad understanding of our business and a network of people across function you will plan your rotation together with your host manager to enhance your development in the best possible way the programme also adapts to the need of the business therefore the project and task vary from rotation to rotation a we are a global company many of our graduate can also go abroad one of their rotation what else is in it you you will be given real task and responsibility with high exposure from day one we believe this is the best way to kick start your career after successfully completing the programme you will continue your career in demant in a permanent position we a flat organization which help you to get a holistic overview of our business to easier find your way around former graduate will partner up with you to support you we furthermore offer you training session such a project and stakeholder management skill we also offer a mentoring scheme which will focus on your personal development besides that you will join a fantastic network with the other graduate whereby everybody grows together already after the first day your business area global business in demant we the full value chain from idea and development to direct sale to our user a a graduate in global business you will work within our largest business where we are responsible operating a leading global hearing aid retailer our headquarters in smørum you will be a part of a highly dedicated and specialized team with a global outreach where we plan manage and execute a wide range of strategic and day to day activity our international colleague in our own hearing care shop around the world during your time in global business you will explore the company and develop your personal and professional skill through job rotation of month each there is a possibility to one of your rotation one of our location abroad the project you will be responsible will be anchored in current and need driven development and your own competency and interest project and task may include digital marketing analytics financial analysis m a customer journey strategy and it development and deployment we a focus on improving interface between business and it technology and how we on one hand can draw on that to enhance customer experience when they visit our shop and the same time optimize work process our colleague a a graduate you will be included in the day to day operation of the department where you also will direct exposure to top management in demant irrespective of the task one thing is certain you will face a steep learning curve with a high degree of responsibility from day one in our flat organization you will train your analytical strategic and innovative skill you will be exposed to a huge range of project you will be expected to take ownership your decision and to challenge status quo your profile you are about to graduate or graduated no more than two year ago with a master s degree in finance economics it accounting or strategy preferably a cand merc cand oecon or similar regardless of your educational background you a good commercial and technological understanding and want to explore the opportunity to optimize process through it you are a top performer with excellent achievement in either your study through your work experience or extracurricular activity you furthermore gained international experience through a semester or internship abroad or similar and last you are fluent in english a a person we believe that you are a team player with a high drive and passion what you do you are curious hardworking and just a important you are humble and fun to work with you are both strategic and pragmatic and go the ambitious goal how graduate programme about u welcome to demant s graduate programme we offer you a career in a global medical healthcare company where you can look forward to an open and fun work environment a look our graduate film to get a first impression demant graduate programme youtube about demant demant is an international leading c company within hearing healthcare we operate in a global market with company in more than country our product are sold in more than country and we employee worldwide demant generates an annual revenue of dkk billion and cover five business activity hearing instrument hearing implant diagnostic equipment hearing care and personal communication about the programme the demant graduate programme offer you a unique opportunity to develop your personal and professional skill each year we hire between graduate different business area we will lead you through a two year journey starting in september depending on the business area you will different rotation each lasting month this will provide you with a broad understanding of our business and a network of people across function you will plan your rotation together with your host manager to enhance your development in the best possible way the programme also adapts to the need of the business therefore the project and task vary from rotation to rotation a we are a global company many of our graduate can also go abroad one of their rotation what else is in it you you will be given real task and responsibility with high exposure from day one we believe this is the best way to kick start your career after successfully completing the programme you will continue your career in demant in a permanent position we a flat organization which help you to get a holistic overview of our business to easier find your way around former graduate will partner up with you to support you we furthermore offer you training session such a project and stakeholder management skill we also offer a mentoring scheme which will focus on your personal development besides that you will join a fantastic network with the other graduate whereby everybody grows together already after the first day your business area global business in demant we the full value chain from idea and development to direct sale to our user a a graduate in global business you will work within our largest business where we are responsible operating a leading global hearing aid retailer our headquarters in smørum you will be a part of a highly dedicated and specialized team with a global outreach where we plan manage and execute a wide range of strategic and day to day activity our international colleague in our own hearing care shop around the world during your time in global business you will explore the company and develop your personal and professional skill through job rotation of month each there is a possibility to one of your rotation one of our location abroad the project you will be responsible will be anchored in current and need driven development and your own competency and interest project and task may include digital marketing analytics financial analysis m a customer journey strategy and it development and deployment we a focus on improving interface between business and it technology and how we on one hand can draw on that to enhance customer experience when they visit our shop and the same time optimize work process our colleague a a graduate you will be included in the day to day operation of the department where you also will direct exposure to top management in demant irrespective of the task one thing is certain you will face a steep learning curve with a high degree of responsibility from day one in our flat organization you will train your analytical strategic and innovative skill you will be exposed to a huge range of project you will be expected to take ownership your decision and to challenge status quo your profile you are about to graduate or graduated no more than two demant meet our employee graduate programme about u welcome to demant s graduate programme we offer you a career in a global medical healthcare company where you can look forward to an open and fun work environment a look our graduate film to get a first impression demant graduate programme youtube about demant demant is an international leading c company within hearing healthcare we operate in a global market with company in more than country our product are sold in more than country and we employee worldwide demant generates an annual revenue of dkk billion and cover five business activity hearing instrument hearing implant diagnostic equipment hearing care and personal communication about the programme the demant graduate programme offer you a unique opportunity to develop your personal and professional skill each year we hire between graduate different business area we will lead you through a two year journey starting in september depending on the business area you will different rotation each lasting month this will provide you with a broad understanding of our business and a network of people across function you will plan your rotation together with your host manager to enhance your development in the best possible way the programme also adapts to the need of the business therefore the project and task vary from rotation to rotation a we are a global company many of our graduate can also go abroad one of their rotation what else is in it you you will be given real task and responsibility with high exposure from day one we believe this is the best way to kick start your career after successfully completing the programme you will continue your career in demant in a permanent position we a flat organization which help you to get a holistic overview of our business to easier find your way around former graduate will partner up with you to support you we furthermore offer you training session such a project and stakeholder management skill we also offer a mentoring scheme which will focus on your personal development besides that you will join a fantastic network with the other graduate whereby everybody grows together already after the first day your business area global business in demant we the full value chain from idea and development to direct sale to our user a a graduate in global business you will work within our largest business where we are responsible operating a leading global hearing aid retailer our headquarters in smørum you will be a part of a highly dedicated and specialized team with a global outreach where we plan manage and execute a wide range of strategic and day to day activity our international colleague in our own hearing care shop around the world during your time in global business you will explore the company and develop your personal and professional skill through job rotation of month each there is a possibility to one of your rotation one of our location abroad the project you will be responsible will be anchored in current and need driven development and your own competency and interest project and task may include digital marketing analytics financial analysis m a customer journey strategy and it development and deployment we a focus on improving interface between business and it technology and how we on one hand can draw on that to enhance customer experience when they visit our shop and the same time optimize work process our colleague a a graduate you will be included in the day to day operation of the department where you also will direct exposure to top management in demant irrespective of the task one thing is certain you will face a steep learning curve with a high degree of responsibility from day one in our flat organization you will train your analytical strategic and innovative skill you will be exposed to a huge range of project you will be expected to take ownership your decision and to challenge status quo your profile you are about to graduate or graduated no more than two year ago with a master s degree in finance economics it accounting or strategy preferably a cand merc cand oecon or similar regardless of your educational background you a good commercial and technological understanding and want to explore the opportunity to optimize process through it you are a top performer with excellent achievement in either your study through your work experience or extracurricular activity you furthermore gained international experience through a semester or internship abroad or similar and last you are fluent in english a a person we believe that you are a team player with a high drive and passion what you do you are curious hardworking and just a important you are humble and fun to work with you are both graduate programme about u welcome to demant s graduate programme we offer you a career in a global medical healthcare company where you can look forward to an open and fun work environment a look our graduate film to get a first impression demant graduate programme youtube about demant demant is an international leading c company within hearing healthcare we operate in a global market with company in more than country our product are sold in more than country and we employee worldwide demant generates an annual revenue of dkk billion and cover five business activity hearing instrument hearing implant diagnostic equipment hearing care and personal communication about the programme the demant graduate programme offer you a unique opportunity to develop your personal and professional skill each year we hire between graduate different business area we will lead you through a two year journey starting in september depending on the business area you will different rotation each lasting month this will provide you with a broad understanding of our business and a network of people across function you will plan your rotation together with your host manager to enhance your development in the best possible way the programme also adapts to the need of the business therefore the project and task vary from rotation to rotation a we are a global company many of our graduate can also go abroad one of their rotation what else is in it you you will be given real task and responsibility with high exposure from day one we believe this is the best way to kick start your career after successfully completing the programme you will continue your career in demant in a permanent position we a flat organization which help you to get a holistic overview of our business to easier find your way around former graduate will partner up with you to support you we furthermore offer you training session such a project and stakeholder management skill we also offer a mentoring scheme which will focus on your personal development besides that you will join a fantastic network with the other graduate whereby everybody grows together already after the first day your business area global business in demant we the full value chain from idea and development to direct sale to our user a a graduate in global business you will work within our largest business where we are responsible operating a leading global hearing aid retailer our headquarters in smørum you will be a part of a highly dedicated and specialized team with a global outreach where we plan manage and execute a wide range of strategic and day to day activity our international colleague in our own hearing care shop around the world during your time in global business you will explore the company and develop your personal and professional skill through job rotation of month each there is a possibility to one of your rotation one of our location abroad the project you will be responsible will be anchored in current and need driven development and your own competency and interest project and task may include digital marketing analytics financial analysis m a customer journey strategy and it development and deployment we a focus on improving interface between business and it technology and how we on one hand can draw on that to enhance customer experience when they visit our shop and the same time opportunity senior business finance partner to human health requisition id posted accounting finance controlling permanent fulltime job posting country job posting location job description print preview apply save job email job to friend return to list location denmark hoersholm country denmark the team you to join you will be a part of business finance which ensures a link between the chr hansen business and financial reporting estimate and performance management business finance is a dedicated team which report to the cfo but is closely integrated into the various business area we aim to drive value creation across chr hansen and to deliver timely and actionable business insight through a proactive and customer focused nature you will be business partner to human health the largest business within health nutrition which is approximately of chr hansen s revenue the role entail a close collaboration with the human health leadership team of which you will be a part what would your role look like you will support the human health leadership team on a day to day basis in the task listed below while maintaining a connection to the finance organization you should be customer centric a cfo mindset and be prepared to speak your mind backed up by fact and data the role is quite dynamic and what you up working with any particular day might be different from what you had planned in the morning responsibility a senior business finance partner to human health act a a constructive and proactive sparring partner to the svp human health and the human health leadership team ensure high quality performance management following up on business case reporting on sale capacity cost dso and capex lead budget forecast monthly review process and annual incentive target setting in alignment with corporate process perform hoc task including but not limited to sparring on business case review new product pipeline project management and steering committee participation being an active partner to the business during completion of commercial contract and pricing lead the financial process human health during strategy update make thing happen with focus on building lasting relationship across the organization through collaboration seek constructive and active participation in the development of the finance business partnering delivery model in chr hansen incl optimization of existing process and solid relationship internal stakeholder in finance it supply operation and r d who are we looking the work environment is dynamic and requires superior interpersonal and communication skill an eye detail and project management skill we are looking a well organized self starter with the ability to prioritize among multiple task a chr hansen will grow significantly the coming year we look someone who is able to develop scalable solution and method to cope with this change finally we are looking a person who seek success through the team s success who is ambitious and willing to walk the extra mile when needed and who understands how to get the best out of colleague without the authority finally it is essential that you a passion human health qualification you a master s degree in business administration finance or economics cand merc cand oecon mba etc academic result and least year of work experience up to date professional finance skill preferably with experience working with sap bi superuser of microsoft office in particular excel and ppt team player who is able to both see the bigger picture and to get into the weed when necessary proven record of great problem solving skill and getting thing done through working with others result driven and keen on delivering high quality output curious and with a desire a paced learning curve and thrive on working independently in new and multiple area the same time ambition to develop into a people leader time is a benefit enjoy working internationally and with different culture striving continuous business improvement together with the team excellent communication skill and you must a proficiency in english both in writing and orally knowledge of danish is a bonus but not a necessity if you these qualification we offer you to be a part of an exciting organization with lot of challenge and competent and motivated colleague what we offer we offer a collaborative informal and dynamic work environment with focus on result if you can deliver excellent work on the agreed deadline we are very flexible when it come how you prefer to plan your day joining chr hansen is your opportunity to make a meaningful difference while unfolding your career in a truly global setting our founder christian d a hansen wa an entrepreneur and that mentality is still very present and valued today a we look new talent to strengthen our team we believe that engagement matter every one of our global office offer an agile organization proud to promote an inspiring work environment and a collaborative culture with the passion to make a difference you will be an important part of a hard working team servicing the business and you will the opportunity to develop your skill and grow with the job if you need more information if you any question please contact senior director martin riise head of business finance health nutrition phone deadline application is january th however application will be reviewed a received about chr hansen chr hansen is a global differentiated bioscience company that develops natural ingredient solution the food nutritional pharmaceutical and agricultural industry chr hansen we are uniquely positioned to drive positive change through microbial solution we worked year to enable sustainable agriculture better food and healthier living more people around the world our microbial and fermentation technology platform including our broad and collection of around microbial strain game changing potential we come far on our journey and delivered result and a we continue to unlock the power of good bacteria through new technology there is so much more we can do our employee are the driving force enabling u to live our mission to pioneer microbial science to improve food health and productivity we work passionately because we know we can make a difference people animal and plant and ultimately our planet innovating a sustainable future is part of our culture our history and our strategy and is embedded in our purpose to grow a better world naturally apply save job email job to friend return to list email this job
